 a mountain or mountain is a naturally elevated part of the earth
 ye zyaadaatar aakasmik tareeke se ubhara hota he

 utpatti ke anusaar parvat chaar prakaar ke hote hai:(a) block parvat (block mountain)-jab chattaanon main sthit bhransh ke kaaran madhya bhaag neeche dhans jaataa he or agal-bagal ke bhaag oonche uthe lagate hai, to wo block parvat kehalaate hai
 The sunken section in the middle is called the Rift Valley
 in parvaton ke sheersh samtal or kinare teevr bhransh-kagaaron se simit hote hai

 jaise- vindhyaachal or satapura, nilgiri, parasnath, rajmahal kii pahadiyaan (bharat), siyara (spain), gaisa or boote (america)(c) sanchit parvat (accumulated mountain)-bhupatal par mitti, baaluu, kankad, pathar lava ke ek sthaan par jamaa hote rahane ke kaaran banane vaala parvat sanchit parvat kehalaata he
 Sand stupas built in the desert fall into this category
 (d) valit parvat (fold mountain)-ye prithvi kii aantarik shaktiyon se dharaatal kii chattaanon ke mud jane se banate hai

 jaise- himalay, alps ural, rockies or andies
